searchaux" style="display:none">List of notable individuals who died in 2018</div>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p><p>The following deaths of notable individuals occurred in 2018. Names are reported under the date of death, in alphabetical order by surname or pseudonym.\n</p><p>A typical entry reports information in the following sequence:\n</p>\n<ul><li>Name, age, country of citizenship at birth, subsequent <a href="/wiki/Nationality" title="Nationality">nationality</a> (if applicable), what subject was noted for, cause of death (if known), and reference.</li></ul>\n<div
